if (!is_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt') != '7cbd1b22170bccd0d1bdc913a0b3e212c8221176') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt') !== '7cbd1b22170bccd0d1bdc913a0b3e212c8221176') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt') !== 'b8a8f9c0ee7689ad31e8585b2d9ebf5d059a30b0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_alpine_linux.txt') !== '7cbd1b22170bccd0d1bdc913a0b3e212c8221176') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/install_alpine_linux.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'd80dc76e926b2e779887419d0923c2136341ec60') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd80dc76e926b2e779887419d0923c2136341ec60') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '81e84e88af647338c8462b4109dbc4d0fae1a733') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd80dc76e926b2e779887419d0923c2136341ec60') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 724\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 724') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
